<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обездолить.html>обездо́ливший</a> (14913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обезоружить.html>обезору́жить</a> (21961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">без-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bez-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orúžije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weapon, arms</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or equivalently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">безору́ж(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bezorúž(nyj)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unarmed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обезоружить.html>обезору́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obezorúžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обезоруживать.html>обезору́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disarm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to calm (an angry person)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безумие.html>безу́мие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bezúmije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-etʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обезуметь.html>обезу́меть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obezúmetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become insane, to go crazy, to go mad</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">обезьꙗна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obezĭjana</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بوزینه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buzine</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">simian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***обернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a> (11205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обёртывать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обора́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wrap up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obernútʹ</b> knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a paper cover on a book</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wind <i>(around)</i>, to wrap <i>(around)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокруг.html>вокру́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льца</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obernútʹ vokrúg pálʹca</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to coax someone into doing what one likes, twist someone around one's little finger</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obernútʹ</b> licó (k)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn one's face (towards)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льзу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obernútʹ</b> vsjó v svojú pólʹzu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn everything to one's profit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obernútʹ</b> vsjó v šútku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn everything into a joke</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn over</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrange, to get done</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folklore</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><i>This term needs a translation to English. Please help out and <b>add a translation</b>, then remove the text <code> |  | rfdef |  | </code>.</i></li></ol>

***обернуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обернуться.html>оберну́ться</a> (1199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воротить.html>вороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуться.html>оберну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборачиваться.html>обора́чиваться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обёртываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wrap oneself (with, in)</li>
<li>to turn head; to turn head backward; to twist round head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́деть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуться.html>оберну́лся</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I tam, gde jevó užé niktó ne mog uvídetʹ, on <b>obernúlsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And where nobody could see him, he <b>turned around</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn (into something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">folklore</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> (+ <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> + accusative case; instrumental case (no presposition))
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тогда.html>тогда́</a> ива́н-царе́вич <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуться.html>оберну́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волк.html>во́лком</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I togdá Iván-carévič <b>obernúlsja</b> vólkom.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And then Ivan-tsarevitch (the prince) <b>turned</b> into a wolf</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to manage, to get by; to wangle</li>
<li>to (go and) come back; (finance) to make a full circle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миг.html>ми́гом</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуться.html>оберну́сь</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja mígom <b>obernúsʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'll go and come back in no time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обернуть.html>оберну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***обертка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обертка.html>обёртка</a> (16625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оберт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obert-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обертка.html>обёртка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">objórtka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обертка.html>обёртки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обертка.html>обёртки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обертка.html>обёрток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wrapper, wrapping</li></ol>

***обескуражить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обескуражить.html>обескура́жить</a> (15133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кураж.html>кура́ж</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kuráž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обескуражить.html>обескура́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obeskurážitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обескура́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to confuse, to perplex, to baffle</li>
<li>to discourage, to dishearten, to dispirit</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечение.html>обеспечение</a> (4422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечить.html>обеспе́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obespéčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ение</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (without stress shift) or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечить.html>обеспе́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obespéčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (with stress shift).

***обеспечиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечиваться.html>обеспе́чиваться</a> (16768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечивать.html>обеспе́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obespéčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечиваться.html>обеспе́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obespéčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обеспе́читься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to provide oneself <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечивать.html>обеспе́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obespéčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
